<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отповедь.html>о́тповедь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótpovedʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отповедь.html>о́тповеди</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отповедь.html>о́тповеди</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отповедь.html>о́тповедей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отправлять.html>отправля́ть</a> (4472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otprávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправлять.html>отправля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otpravljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send, to dispatch, to forward
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отправлять.html>отправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:праотец.html>праотца́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpravljátʹ</b> k praotcám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kill, to send smb. to kingdom come</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отправлять.html>отправля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:естественный.html>есте́ственные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надобность.html>на́добности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otpravljátʹ</b> jestéstvennyje nádobnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ease nature (<i>euphemism</i>)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exercise, to perform, to discharge</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпрыск.html>о́тпрыск</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ótprysk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпрыск.html>о́тпрыска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпрыск.html>о́тпрыски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отпрыск.html>о́тпрысков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> offshoot</li>
